What Makes The Zero Gravity So Special?


Zero Gravity fly rods use the same composite system that√É¬¢Ä√¢ÄÔøΩafter five years√É¬¢Ä√¢ÄÔøΩ the US Army found made a dramatic difference in Apache helicopter blades.Zero G Fly Rods: Using the same technology as Blackhawk II Helicoper blades You might think it√É¬¢Ä√¢‚Äû¬¢s a stretch between rotor blades and fly rods, but they both require similar properties. Helicopter blades undergo constant turbulence, far more than an airplane√É¬¢Ä√¢‚Äû¬¢s wings, yet they must be light, strong, and flexible. Not too far from what a fly rod has to put up with during a blitz of tuna. The US Army found that by making Apache blades from graphite composites with thermoplastic-enriched thermoset resins, the blades could produce a larger airfoil, rotate at higher speeds, and carry a bigger payload at the same time making it four times stronger!

These composites are also used in the V-22 Osprey, C-17 transport planes, the F-22 fighterScientist who helped formuate the Zero G Fly Rod, the Joint Strike Fighter, and the top-secret UCAV (Unmanned Combat Aerial Vehicle). Our exclusive consultant on fly rod materials is a composite scientist with top security clearance. The new Zero G fly rods are a result of his research with the military and our testing of fly rods using this technology in the field.
What makes them so special?

Thermoplastic Resins

Only three fly rod series in the world exist that use high-cure thermoplastic enriched thermoset resins: Orvis Zero Gravity, Orvis T-3, and Orvis TLS Power Matrix. Our exclusive resins are set at a high cure temperature, and completely encase the graphite fibers used as the main source of power, distance, and accuracy in a fly rod. In contrast to the standard epoxy resins found in all other fly rods, thermoplastics make a fly rod stronger, tougher, and more accurate.

Boron Fibers in our Strategic Positioning System

Boron is a stiff, strong, and very expensive fiber. Alone, it√É¬¢Ä√¢‚Äû¬¢s too stiff to make a fly rod by conventional means. But, when we add just the right amount of boron into the butt section of a rod it produces a reserve power, because boron compresses less under stress. This power takes over in your longest casts or when playing big fish with maximum stress on the rod. Plus, our new Strategic Positioning System, developed specifically for Zero Gravity rods, allows us to place the boron fibers in precisely the right spot and in just the right amount for each individual rod taper.

Unidirectional Carbon Scrim

Did you know fiberglass is used in most all other graphite rods?The Latest in Scrim Technology Graphite and resins by themselves don√É¬¢Ä√¢‚Äû¬¢t offer enough strength to withstand normal fishing conditions. So, a supportive layer of fiberglass is attached to the graphite fibers before they√É¬¢Ä√¢‚Äû¬¢re wrapped around a steel mandrel to form the taper. It√É¬¢Ä√¢‚Äû¬¢s worked well for 30 years, but it adds weight to a rod. Our Zero G rods use the latest in scrim technology: Unidirectional graphite scrim, which is lighter, stronger, and more dependable than fiberglass scrim. Because this material, part of our Strategic Positioning System, is so strong we only need to use a fraction of the graphite, as compared to the fiberglass used in other rods. The result is a much thinner rod yet even stronger fly rod.

Some other rod manufacturers claim to use graphite scrim in their rods, but many use a mat of graphite fibers, which doesnt offer the strength and superior fiber alignment (and thus better rod tracking you get by using unidirectional graphite scrim.

The Bottom Line:

Zero G rod blanks are 25% stronger yet 25% thinner than comparable blanks, and 40% lighter.
If youre totally satisfied with your casting, have no worries about your rod breaking on the trip of a lifetime, and can put the fly exactly where you want it every time, you probably dont need a Zero G. But, if you√É¬¢Ä√¢‚Äû¬¢re not always happy with your casting, the Zero G technology is the best reason you√É¬¢Ä√¢‚Äû¬¢ll ever have to upgrade.

 

Questions? Call Us 800.201.2557

To guarantee the level of dependability\r\nconsumers have come to expect from all Ross products, we have designed\r\na drag system for the Evolution series that has triple redundancy;\r\nproviding for three backup drag systems and thereby guaranteeing\r\ndependability under the most demanding fishing conditions. The spoke\r\ndesigned frame and extensive spool ventilation make this series\r\nincredibly lightweight, yet the Evolution is built to endure a lifetime\r\nof flawless performance. The Evolution series is truly art\r\nin motion, and will satisfy the demands of the most discriminating\r\nangler.

    Mo men tum: (mO-'men-tm) (n. pl.) - A measure of the motion of a body equal to the product of its mass and velocity.

    \r\n

    Synonyms: drive, energy, power, strength

    \r\n \r\n \r\n

    The\r\nMomentum reel series has proven to be the strongest and most dependable\r\nsaltwater fly reel on the water today, and is a perfect example of how\r\nto maximize the benefits of carbon fiber technology in a drag system.\r\nStiffness, strength, heat resistance, shock-dampening capabilities and\r\ninfinite fatigue resistance are all properties of carbon fiber that\r\nhelp make the Momentum drag system the strongest and most dependable\r\nbig game reel available. We have partnered with Kestrel Bike Company in\r\nthe development of the Momentum's carbon fiber drag system. Our vast\r\nexperience in fly reel design and manufacturing is equally matched by\r\nKestrel's expertise in the design and production of carbon fiber\r\ncomponents. Kestrel has been manufacturing the world's finest carbon\r\nfiber bikes since 1987. In fact, Kestrel designed and produced the very\r\nfirst all-carbon bike frame. They are pioneers in the carbon fiber\r\nindustry and we were thrilled that a company of their caliber agreed to\r\njoin us in the development of this new drag technology. When it comes\r\nto engineering, development and production of carbon fiber products,\r\nKestrel has written the book and their expertise with carbon fiber is\r\nsimply unmatched.

    \r\n

    Welcome to the next generation of Ross\r\nproducts! The Momentum series represents a cosmic departure from\r\ncurrent Ross designs in both function and style. The carbon fiber we\r\nhave employed for the Momentum drag system is incredibly strong! The\r\nmeasurement of the strength for this material is ""ksi"", which denotes\r\ntensile strength in thousands of pounds per square inch. So just how\r\nstrong is our carbon fiber drag system? To get a good perspective on\r\nthis, the aluminum used to produce Ross products is 45ksi; meaning it\r\ncan resist a tension load of 45,000 pounds per square inch of material.\r\nThis is pretty impressive until you realize that the carbon fiber used\r\nin the Momentum drag system is 700ksi - vastly stronger than aluminum,\r\nsteel and even titanium!

    \r\n

    The first time you handle a Momentum\r\nreel, you will be amazed with its meticulous machining and ergonomic\r\ndesign. We have custom fit this series with a large, well positioned\r\ndrag knob - easily found for adjustment during the heat of battle, but\r\nnever in the way. Additionally, the Momentum's handle has been designed\r\nto fit comfortably between your fingers, but will never slip free when\r\ntaking on a monster fish. Each reel in this series is designed with a\r\nspecific diameter and width to maximize the properties of drag\r\nconsistency and quick line retrieval. With 6.3 square inches of\r\neffective drag surface, and 12 pounds of dead lift weight, the Momentum\r\nseries has three times the effective stopping power of every drag\r\ntested. Put simply, the Momentum is the strongest fly fishing reel on\r\nthe market today; and it costs considerably less than many competitive\r\nbrands. A triple redundancy drag system ensures dependability under the\r\nmost demanding fishing conditions, and by adding in features like\r\ntitanium drag components, a quick-release locking spool and water\r\nshedding grooves on the palming rim, you have the ultimate big game fly\r\nreel. With a wide range of sizes available, the Momentum series is\r\nappropriate for any fishing application, including Spey.

    The Flystart is a hybrid large arbor fly reel that is inexpensive, yet built with the same commitment to quality and performance as all Ross reels. The drag system is designed to be smooth, consistent and have a wide range of adjustment. Fly fishing is a sport that everyone can enjoy, but for many people, the price of fly tackle is often a barrier to participation. The Ross team was committed to producing an introductory priced fly reel that would perform to the expectations of even the most experienced angler, and the Flystart series perfectly meets this goal. You will be amazed with its quality in manufacturing tolerance, drag performance and sound. The Flystart is a great reel for first-time fly fishing participants that demand quality, but do not want to spend a fortune gearing up to fish.

    The Flystart series come with the following standard features:

    • Manufactured out of high quality aluminum
    • Self-lubricating, synthetic drag system that is virtually maintenance free
    • Electrostatically coated for the perfect balance of hardness and color
    • Seamless transition between line-in and drag engagement (no start-up friction)
    • Quick release locking spool
    • Easy left-hand to right-hand retrieve conversion
    • Exposed spool rim for palming

    FRAME/SPOOL MATERIAL High quality aluminum alloy

    MANUFACTURING SPECIFICATIONS Gravity fed - cast aluminum, 1 piece frame, 2 piece assembled spool, machine finished

    DRAG MATERIAL 500P √ÉÔøΩ space-age polymer that is durable, heat resistant, self-lubricating and maintenance free

    DRAG ENGAGEMENT SYSTEM Delrin 500P interface √ÉÔøΩ offset gear-to-gear disc drag engagement

    ESCAPEMENT SYSTEM Pawl engagement

    SPOOL ROTATION MECHANISM Oil impregnated bronze bushings rotating on a stainless steel spindle

    FINISH Corrosion resistant electrostatic coating

    NUMBER OF REELS IN SERIES 4

    FLY ROD COVERAGE 3wt. - 8wt.

    FISHING APPLICATION Designed for use in all freshwater and saltwater fishing environments

    The Flystart is a hybrid large arbor fly reel that is inexpensive, yet built with the same commitment to quality and performance as all Ross reels. The drag system is designed to be smooth, consistent and have a wide range of adjustment. Fly fishing is a sport that everyone can enjoy, but for many people, the price of fly tackle is often a barrier to participation. The Ross team was committed to producing an introductory priced fly reel that would perform to the expectations of even the most experienced angler, and the Flystart series perfectly meets this goal. You will be amazed with its quality in manufacturing tolerance, drag performance and sound. The Flystart is a great reel for first-time fly fishing participants that demand quality, but do not want to spend a fortune gearing up to fish.

    The Flystart series come with the following standard features:

    • Manufactured out of high quality aluminum
    • Self-lubricating, synthetic drag system that is virtually maintenance free
    • Electrostatically coated for the perfect balance of hardness and color
    • Seamless transition between line-in and drag engagement (no start-up friction)
    • Quick release locking spool
    • Easy left-hand to right-hand retrieve conversion
    • Exposed spool rim for palming

    The Zephyr Carbon Fiber Series of landing nets are 100% carbon fiber, molded nets. Extremely light in weight, (they float like corks), but tough enough to withstand all the elements that you put up with when fishing, whether you are wading, float tubing, or in a boat. Designed and tested on the blue ribbon waters of the US and the World, Zephyrs are the landing nets you and Fly Fishing Team USA can count on time and time again.

    Zephyr
    A 100% carbon fiber personal landing net with an offset handle that reduces or eliminates the need to angle one's wrist when landing a fish. The bow size and the net bag combine to accommodate fish up to 24"". Comes standard with the Snake River Sling, a lanyard that doubles as a carrier and an 8"" deep NoSnagBag2. Fly Fishing Team USA depended on a Zephyr, shouldn't you?

    Dimensions:
    Bow 9.5""x 16"" Overall length 23""

    LZ-1
    The LZ-1 is the smaller cousin to the Zephyr. The LZ-1 has the same offset handle as the Zephyr and also comes standard with the Snake River Sling. Fish up to 18"" will fit in this landing net with an 8"" deep NoSnagBag2.

    Dimensions:
    Bow 8.5""x 13"" Overall length 19.75""

    BZ-6
    The BZ-6 has the shortest handle (6"") in the BZ series. This net is great for those whose wade and want to carry a larger net on their back for the big cutthroats, rainbows, browns or steelhead they are stalking. Synthetic leather grip, hanger cap and Snake River Sling are standard. Offered with a 10"" deep NoSnagBag2.

    Dimensions:
    Bow 12"" x20"" Overall length 26""


    BZ-12
    The BZ-12 is designed for the float tuber. The BZ-12's overall length is 32"", which gives the tuber plenty of reach for landing fish, but isn't too long to get in the way. Synthetic leather grip, hanger end cap and a 10"" deep NoSnagBag2 are standard.

    Dimensions:
    Bow 12"" x20"" Overall length 32""

    BZ-28
    The BZ-28 has the same head size as the BZ-12, but comes with a 28"" handle. The lightweight net that is perfect for smaller drift boats, pontoons, canoes, or prams. Guides who take clients on walk-in trips to spring creeks love this net due to its reach, fish-friendly, flat bottom, nylon net bag and its light weight. Synthetic leather grip, hanger end cap and a 10"" deep NoSnagBag2 are standard.
    Dimensions:
    Bow 12"" x20"" Overall length 48""

    Howard Croston, the specialist product adviser and England Team \r\n Member, explains exactly what we were trying to achieve with the Angel.

    \r\n

    ""Our objectives were to make the lightest, most responsive rod ever \r\n made. We wanted a rod that could deliver great performance with a minimum \r\n of effort. And that‚Äôs what we‚Äôve done. The Angel gives great loop \r\n formation, and you can point, lift and shoot out a line with bull‚Äôs-eye \r\n accuracy. It is as close as we can get to that indescribable buzz you feel \r\n when you pick up a rod that you know instantly is made for you. The Angel \r\n isn‚Äôt just physically light ‚Äì we‚Äôve shaved half an ounce \r\n off virtually every other comparable fl y rod in
    \r\n the world - but it feels light.""

    \r\n

    ""So, we‚Äôve built the best rod in the world. Where did we go from \r\n there? Well, to the guides and the ghillies of the world. We put the Angel \r\n through a whole year of trials in every conceivable climate and water type \r\n - for fish big and small. Long casting. Short casting. Baking hot or freezing \r\n cold, the Angel has been there and done it. I‚Äôve lived with the rod \r\n for well over a year and it‚Äôs truly great. I love it. Definitely my favorite rod.‚Äù

    \r\n

    We also realize that the best rod in the world deserves to see the world \r\n so we‚Äôve built a multi-piece Smuggler version. This breaks down into \r\n a rod tube short enough to fit into any suitcase, holdall or aircraft locker \r\n so that you never need to go anywhere without your guardian Angel.

    \r\n

    The\r\nAngel has won a host of awards and received fantastic reviews world\r\nwide. It's the most talked about range for years. The hope we had for\r\nit during its development have been more than realized. Its lightness\r\nand fast tip action gives incomparable loop formation. You can point,\r\nlift and shoot out a line with unerring accuracy.

    ZANE FLY ROD SERIES

    \r\n

    Hardy has a rich tradition\r\nof building innovative tackle for saltwater fishing and eighty years\r\nago Zane Grey, the famous American author, angler and traveler was a\r\nfriend of the company. We designed much of his tackle for many of his\r\nexploratory angling trips around the seas of the world. After a great\r\ndeal of testing and even more feedback, we are convinced that the new\r\nZane range of saltwater fly rods is going to prove a worthy tribute to\r\none of angling‚Äôs great pioneers.

    \r\n

    The key to the Zane rods are\r\nthe blanks, amongst the slimmest ever produced, capable of cutting\r\nthrough coastal winds like a knife. A careful blend of multi-modulus\r\nfibers allows easy loading but very fast recovery ‚Äì the perfect\r\ncombination for quick accurate casting over any range.

    \r\n

    On the\r\nbutt section are two Fuji-lines SIC rings, one of 20mm and one of 16mm.\r\nThese are designed to allow super-rapid line clearance and to funnel\r\nthe line for that last powerful shoot.

    \r\n

    The reel seat is\r\nhard-anodized aluminum, picked out in blue, to mirror the color of the\r\nblanks and to match the trim of the Zane reels. The double locking\r\nscrews clamp the reel to the rod ‚Äì but the fitted nylon washers mean it\r\nwon‚Äôt be stuck there at the end of the day!

    \r\n

    Zane rods are\r\ndesigned for saltwater fishing but are also ideal for other species\r\nlike salmon, sea-trout, steelhead and even pike.

    \r\n

    The fine\r\npoints of the Zane package include carved aluminum stoppers, a glass\r\nreinforced carbon tube in translucent blue, and elegantly etched rod\r\ndetails. The Zane is supplied in a protective neoprene carrying system.

    \r\n

    All the rods are 9‚Äô in length.

    \r\n
    • \r\nThe #7 is a light bonefish rod for those calm days when presentation is\r\nparamount. It is also ideal for sea trout and sea bass in northern\r\nEurope.
    • The #8 is the mainstay bonefish rod, an all around saltwater classic.
    • The #9 is perfect for smaller permit and the biggest bonefish.
    • The #10 is the permit rod par-excellence and ideal for medium tarpon.
    • The #12 is the ideal rod for handling tarpon, shark and other blue water species.
    \r\n

    Swift MK II Fly Rod Series \r\n

    \r\n

    The quality of\r\nmaterials, the design and make-up, together with a beautiful silver\r\nfinish have combined to make the Swift MkII a serious performer on the\r\nworld stage. Especially so when considering the cost. Firm, powerful\r\nactions suit the angler with a quick precise casting style. Many of\r\nthese Swift aficionados are competition anglers, or at least those who\r\nfish reservoirs and large stillwaters. The Swift can throw a tight\r\ncontrolled loop with ease, hook and hold a mature grown-on rainbow yet\r\nstill effortlessly roll cast a short line when required. This supreme\r\nadaptability provides an ideal solution to every problem the\r\nexperienced stillwater angler will ever face.

    Of course, if you partner the Swift MkII rod with the Swift\r\nreel, you'll have a package that will delight the eye and satisfy all\r\nyour angling ambitions for years to come. This Swift range performs at\r\nthe very highest level - and at a price that is very affordable.

    \r\n

    To complete the range, we've introduced two new models for 2007 specifically for the river fisherman.

    \r\n
    • The 8' #4 takes the Swift into the realm of the brook and small chalk stream angler.
    • The new 8' 6"" #5 is slightly quicker with a fraction more power and the ability to turnover big flies in a breeze.

    GLADSTONE (SPLIT BAMBOO)\r\n

    \r\n

    Named\r\nin tribute to Callum Gladstone, our master-builder of split-bamboo fly\r\nrods, the first thing that you will notice about this new rod is its\r\nspectacular appearance. Prior to the building process, the finest\r\nTonkin bamboo is hand-flamed, resulting in a rich, dark brown\r\ntortoiseshell finish.
    \r\n
    This two-piece rod series is\r\navailable in three sizes, each with its own individual taper that\r\ncelebrates the achievements of some of the greatest American split-cane\r\nrod builders of the past: the Leonard family, Everett Garrison and\r\nEdward Payne. Minute adjustments are made to the Hardy precision\r\nplanning form, to painstakingly recreate a modern version of these\r\nclassic tapers. The perfect angle and taper on each spline means that\r\nthe finished rod forms a perfect hexagon. Each rod shares in common the\r\n‚Äòswelled butt‚Äô that contributes considerable backbone to the feel,\r\nallowing a deep action to be combined with excellent dampening\r\ncharacteristics.    \r\n \r\n
